data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="discoverySectionWrapper"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><h2 id="apple-pay-integration" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#apple-pay-integration" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#apple-pay-integration" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Apple Pay integration</h2></div><div style="width:100%" class="discovery-section"><div class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-discoverySection__SD8-t" style="background-color:#fff"><div class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionContainer__hHVxt"><div data-testid="pp-sectionContent"><div data-testid="pp-sectionBlurb" class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionBlurb__nHd0q"><div data-testid="pp-blurb" class="Blurb-module_pp-blurb__lzocM"><h2></h2><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div data-ppui="true" class="css-1nhh7rf-col"><span>
    </span><p><span>Apple Pay is a mobile payment and digital wallet service provided by Apple Inc.</span></p><span>
    </span><p><span>Buyers can use Apple Pay to make payments on the web using the Safari web browser or an iOS device.</span></p><span>
    </span><p><span>Sellers can use Apple Pay to sell:</span></p><span>
    </span><ul><span>
        </span><li><span>Physical goods, such as clothes and electronics.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><span>Digital goods, such as software.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><span>Intangible professional services, such as concerts or gym memberships.</span></li><span>
    </span></ul><span>
    </span><p><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/passkit/apple_pay" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Visit this site</span></a><span> for more information about Apple Pay.</span></p><span>
</span></div><span>
</span></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="pp-sectionImage" class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionImage__BX-KD"><div class="ImageContainer-module_pp-imageContainer__awIei ImageContainer-module_backdrop__ML0hr"><img data-testid="pp-image" src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/ppdevdocs/img/applepay-sheet-xxl-m.png" alt="Apple Pay integration"/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="supported-countries-and-currencies" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="supported-countries-and-currencies" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#supported-countries-and-currencies" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#supported-countries-and-currencies" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Supported countries and currencies</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div data-ppui="true" class="css-1nhh7rf-col"><span>
    </span><p><span>Apple Pay supports payments in 34 countries and 22 currencies:</span></p><span>
    </span><ul><span>
        </span><li><strong><span>Countries:</span></strong><span> Australia, Austria, Belgium, Bulgaria, Canada, China, Cyprus, Czech Republic, Denmark, Estonia, Finland, France, Germany, Greece, Hong Kong, Hungary, Ireland, Italy, Japan, Latvia, Liechtenstein, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Netherlands, Norway, Poland, Portugal, Romania, Singapore, Slovakia, Slovenia, Spain, Sweden, United States, United Kingdom</span></li><span>
        </span><li><strong><span>Currencies:</span></strong><span> </span><code class=""><span>AUD</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>BRL</span></code><span>,
              </span><code class=""><span>CAD</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>CHF</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>CZK</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>DKK</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>EUR</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>GBP</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>HKD</span></code><span>,
              </span><code class=""><span>HUF</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>ILS</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>JPY</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>MXN</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>NOK</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>NZD</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>PHP</span></code><span>,
              </span><code class=""><span>PLN</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>SEK</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>SGD</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>THB</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>TWD</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>USD</span></code><span>
        </span></li><span>
    </span></ul><span>
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div "><span>
    </span><p><span>Apple Pay Recurring for Japan is not supported.</span></p><span>
</span></div></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="how-it-works" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="discoverySectionWrapper"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><h2 id="how-it-works" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#how-it-works" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#how-it-works" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->How it works</h2></div><div style="width:100%" class="discovery-section"><div class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-discoverySection__SD8-t" style="background-color:#fff"><div class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionContainer__hHVxt"><div data-testid="pp-sectionContent"><div data-testid="pp-sectionBlurb" class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionBlurb__nHd0q"><div data-testid="pp-blurb" class="Blurb-module_pp-blurb__lzocM"><h2></h2><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div data-ppui="true" class="css-1nhh7rf-col"><p><span>The Apple Pay button shows up on your website when a customer uses the Safari web browser on an eligible device.</span></p><p><span>When your buyer selects the Apple Pay button:</span></p><ol><li><span>Your website shows the buyer a payment sheet.</span></li><li><span>The buyer confirms the purchase details, such as the shipping address and payment method.</span></li><li><span>The buyer authorizes the purchase on the payment sheet.</span></li></ol><p><span>The payment sheet helps streamline the checkout process by showing the customer the information needed to make the payment.</span></p><p><span>Payment sheets can show the user's name, address, shipping information, and email address. You can customize this payment sheet to include the user details and payment information you need for your Apple Pay integration.</span></p><p><a href="https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT208531" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Visit this site</span></a><span>  for more details about Apple Pay's compatibility.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="pp-sectionImage" class="DiscoverySection-module_pp-sectionImage__BX-KD"><div class="ImageContainer-module_pp-imageContainer__awIei ImageContainer-module_backdrop__ML0hr"><img data-testid="pp-image" src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/ppdevdocs/img/applepay_mobile.png" alt="How it works"/></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="integration-video" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="integration-video" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#integration-video" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#integration-video" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Integration video</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.3" id="link-integrationvideo" class="css-s8u2ug-row"><span>

clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="css-1v4k93a-badge_base-text_caption-warning" data-ppui-info="badge_3.4.10__7.46.3">Required</span></div></h3></header><style data-emotion="css 1soddj9-content">.css-1soddj9-content{margin-top:0.9375rem;margin-bottom:0.9375rem;}</style><div class="css-1soddj9-content" data-ppui="true"><style data-emotion="css 16jt5za-text_body">.css-16jt5za-text_body{color:#001435;font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,"Helvetica Neue",Arial,sans-serif;font-size:1.125rem;line-height:1.5rem;font-weight:400;}@media screen and (max-width: 752px){.css-16jt5za-text_body{font-size:min(1.125rem, 36px);line-height:min(1.5rem, 48px);}}</style><div class="body-text-section css-16jt5za-text_body" data-ppui-info="body-text_6.7.7__7.46.3"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>You must be an approved partner to integrate the Apple Pay SDK.
</span></p><p><span>For customers to pay with Apple Pay, they must be in a region where Apple Pay is supported, and their devices must meet the following requirements:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Device compatibility: The device must support Apple Pay.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>iOS version: iOS 12.1 or later.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Desktop: macOS 10.14.1 or later.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Supported browsers: Safari. With the </span><a href="https://applepay.cdn-apple.com/jsapi/1.latest/apple-pay-sdk.js" class="undefined dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" title="external link"><span>latest Apple Pay SDK</span></a><span>, customers can also pay using non-Safari browsers.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><span>PayPal also provides iframe support for ApplePay. To use ApplePay within an iframe:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>The iframe tag must have the attribute&nbsp;</span><code class=""><span>allow="payment"</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The parent domain hosting the iframe needs to have it's domain validated by following the usual process with PayPal.</span></li><span>
</span></ul></div></div></div><style data-emotion="css 1ygyq7k-footer">.css-1ygyq7k-footer{margin-top:1.5rem;}.css-1ygyq7k-footer button,.css-1ygyq7k-footer a{margin:initial;}.css-1ygyq7k-footer a:not(:last-child){margin-right:initial;margin-left:1.5rem;}</style><footer class="css-1ygyq7k-footer" data-ppui="true"><style data-emotion="css data-ppui-info="card_2.4.8__7.46.3" style="margin-bottom:2rem"><header class="css-1ao4o69-header" style="width:100%" data-ppui="true"><h3 class="css-qczjjc-title-text_heading_sm" data-ppui="true"><div </span><p><span>Currently supports Apple Pay one-time payments with the buyer present.</span><br/></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Review Apple's terms and conditions for the Apple Pay platform.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>See Apple's developer terms for more information.</span></li><span>

class="css-1nhh7rf-col"><span>
    </span><div class="openInCodeSpaces-div"><span>
        </span><p class="open-in-codespaces-module--open_in_codespace__header--1pnpf"><span>Get up and running in GitHub Codespaces</span></p><span>
        </span><p class="open-in-codespaces-module--open_in_codespace__text--2kyec"><span><span>GitHub Codespaces are cloud-based development environments where you can code and test your PayPal integrations. </span></span><a href="/api/rest/sandbox/codespaces/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Learn more</span></a></p><span>
        </span><p><a href="https://github.com/codespaces/new/paypal-examples/applepay" class="undefined dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span><span>Open in Codespaces</span></span></a></p><span>
    </span></div><span>
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="set-up-your-sandbox-account-to-accept-apple-pay" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">1</span><h2 id="set-up-your-sandbox-account-to-accept-apple-pay" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#set-up-your-sandbox-account-to-accept-apple-pay" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#set-up-your-sandbox-account-to-accept-apple-pay" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Set up your sandbox account to accept Apple Pay</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div data-ppui="true" class="css-1nhh7rf-col"><span>
    </span><p><span>Before you can accept Apple Pay on your website, verify that your sandbox business account supports Apple Pay. Use the PayPal Developer Dashboard to set up your sandbox account to accept Apple Pay.</span></p><span>
    </span><ol><span>
        </span><li><span>Log into the </span><a href="/dashboard/applications/sandbox" class="dx-external-href linkFormat dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>PayPal Developer Dashboard</span></a><span> and go to your sandbox account.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><span>Go to </span><strong><span>Apps & Credentials</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><span>Make sure you are in the PayPal sandbox environment by selecting </span><strong><span>Sandbox</span></strong><span> at the top.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><span>Select or create an app.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><span>Scroll down to </span><strong><span>Features</span></strong><span> and check if Apple Pay is enabled. If Apple Pay isn't enabled, select the </span><strong><span> Apple Pay</span></strong><span> checkbox and select the "Save" link to enable Apple Pay.</span></li><span>
    </span></ol><span>
    </span><p><span>If you created a sandbox business account through </span><a href="https://sandbox.paypal.com/" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>sandbox.paypal.com</span></a><span>, and the Apple Pay status for the account shows as disabled, </span><a href="https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/bizsignup/add-product?product=payment_methods&amp;capabilities=APPLE_PAY&amp;_ga=1.255056589.491931369.1702610895" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>complete the sandbox onboarding steps</span></a><span> to enable Apple Pay.</span></p><span>
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><strong><span>Tip: </span></strong><span>When your integration is ready to go live, read the </span><span class="boldArchText"><span>Go live</span></span><span> section for details about the additional steps needed for Apple Pay onboarding.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="getting-started-in-your-testing-environment" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">2</span><h2 id="getting-started-in-your-testing-environment" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#getting-started-in-your-testing-environment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#getting-started-in-your-testing-environment" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Getting started in your testing environment</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><div data-ppui="true" class="css-1nhh7rf-col"><span>
    </span><p><span>Before you develop your Apple Pay on the Web integration, you need to complete
          </span><a href="/api/rest/" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Get started</span></a><span>  to set up your PayPal account, client ID, and sandbox emails for testing.
    </span></p><span>
    </span><ol><span>
        </span><li><strong><span>Download and host</span></strong><span> the domain association file for your sandbox environment.</span></li><span>
        </span><li><strong><span>Register your sandbox domain.</span></strong></li><span>
        </span><li><strong><span>Create an Apple Pay sandbox account</span></strong><span> for testing. You don't need an Apple developer account to go live.</span></li><span>
    </span></ol><span>
    
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><b><span>Important: </span></b><span>You need to verify any domain names that you want to show an Apple Pay button. Apple rejects payments from unverified domains. The Apple Pay payment method won't work if the domain isn't registered.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h2 id="download-and-host-sandbox-domain-association-file" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#download-and-host-sandbox-domain-association-file" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#download-and-host-sandbox-domain-association-file" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> Download and host sandbox domain association file</h2><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Download the domain association file for your sandbox environment.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Host the file on your test environment at </span><code class=""><span>/.well-known/apple-developer-merchantid-domain-association.</span></code></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><a href="https://paypalobjects.com/devdoc/apple-pay/sandbox/apple-developer-merchantid-domain-association" class="css-1m0ekac-button_base-text_button_lg-btn_full_width dx-external-href dx-external-href" role="button" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ppui-info="buttons_7.9.9" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Download</span></a><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><h2 id="register-your-sandbox-domains" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#register-your-sandbox-domains" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#register-your-sandbox-domains" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> Register your sandbox domains</h2><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Go to your PayPal Developer Dashboard.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Register all high-level domains and subdomains that show the Apple Pay button, such as businessexample.com and checkout.businessexample.com.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>After the domains and subdomains are registered, you can test the Apple Pay buttons after you register the domains and subdomains.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="create-apple-pay-sandbox-account" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="create-apple-pay-sandbox-account" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#create-apple-pay-sandbox-account" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#create-apple-pay-sandbox-account" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Create Apple Pay sandbox account</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Create an Apple Pay sandbox account on the Apple Developer website to get a test wallet and test cards to test your Apple Pay integration.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>If you already have an Apple sandbox account, you can use that account and move on to the next step.</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Create an
          </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Apple developer account</span></a><span>.
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Create an
          </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/apple-pay/sandbox-testing/" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Apple sandbox account</span></a><span>.
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Get test cards from your Apple sandbox account.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="integrate-apple-pay-checkout" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3 id="call-the-orders-api" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#call-the-orders-api" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#call-the-orders-api" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> Call the Orders API</h3><span>
</span><p><span>To accept Apple Pay directly on your website, create API endpoints on your server that communicate with the
      </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2/" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>PayPal Orders V2 API</span></a><span>. These endpoints can create an order, authorize payment, and capture payment for an order.
</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="server-side-example-nodejs" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#server-side-example-nodejs" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#server-side-example-nodejs" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-serversideexamplenodejs" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-serversideexamplenodejs" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Server-side example (Node.js)</h3><span>
</span><p><span>The following example uses the
      </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2/" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>PayPal Orders V2 API</span></a><span>  to add routes to an Express server for creating orders and capturing payments.

style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:rgb(78, 201, 176)">script</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">&gt;</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="codeContent"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>PayPal's Apple Pay component interacts with your JavaScript code in 4 areas:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><li><span>Checking merchant eligibility for Apple Pay:  </span><code class=""><span>paypal.Applepay().config()</span></code><span>.</span></li><li><span>Creating an Apple Pay session.</span></li><li><span>Handling the </span><code class=""><span>onvalidatemerchant</span></code><span> callback:  </span><code class=""><span>paypal.Applepay().validateMerchant()</span></code><span>.</span></li><li><span>Handling the </span><code class=""><span>onpaymentauthorized</span></code><span> callback:  </span><code class=""><span>paypal.Applepay().confirmOrder()</span></code><span>.</span></li></ol><span>
</span><p><span>Before you show the Apple Pay button, make sure that you can create an Apple Pay instance and that the device can make an Apple Pay payment.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Use </span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession.canMakePayments</span></code><span> to check if the device can make Apple Pay payments.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><b><span>Tip: </span></b><span>When testing, you need to be logged into the iCloud account for your testing environment. Testing in the sandbox requires you to log into an </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/apple-pay/sandbox-testing/" class="dx-external-href linkFormat dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>iTunes Connect sandbox tester account</span></a><span>, which you can create with an </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/help/account/" class="dx-external-href linkFormat dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Apple Developer account</span></a><span>. When you test in a live environment, log into a live iCloud account.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Check for device and merchant eligibility before setting up the Apple Pay button.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>To check eligibility, use the PayPal JavaScript SDK API  </span><code class=""><span>paypal.Applepay().config()</span></code><span>.</span></p></div><div more details on how to set up the Apple Pay button in  </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/applepayjs/displaying_apple_pay_buttons" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Apple's developer documentation</span></a><span>.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="create-apple-pay-session" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><div class="dx-anchor newArchetype numberedWrapper"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">5</span><h2 id="create-apple-pay-session" class="dx-anchor newArchetype"> <span id="#create-apple-pay-session" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#create-apple-pay-session" class="dx-anchor__icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Create Apple Pay session</h2></div></div></div><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span> object manages the Apple Pay payment process on the web. Create a new </span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span> each time a buyer explicitly requests a payment, such as inside an</span><code class=""><span>onclick</span></code><span> event. If you don't create an</span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span> each time, you get a "Must create a new</span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span> from a user gesture handler" JavaScript exception. For more information about this error, visit Apple's Creating an Apple Pay Session page.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>For each </span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span>, create an</span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/apple_pay_on_the_web/applepaypaymentrequest" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><code class=""><span>ApplePayPaymentRequest</span></code></a><span> object, which includes information about payment processing capabilities, the payment amount, and shipping information.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>The response object of the PayPal JavaScript SDK API  </span><code class=""><span>paypal.Applepay().config()</span></code><span> provides the following parameters in the </span><code class=""><span>ApplePayPaymentRequest</span></code><span> object:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><li><code class=""><span>countryCode</span></code></li><li><code class=""><span>merchantCapabilities</span></code></li><li><code class=""><span>supportedNetworks</span></code></li></ul></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span> inside a gesture handler, such as an </span><code class=""><span>onclick</span></code><span> event or an </span><code class=""><span>addEventListener</span></code><span>  click handler.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Creating an </span><code class=""><span>ApplePaySession</span></code><span> object throws a JavaScript exception if any of the following occurs:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><li><span>Any Apple Pay JavaScript API is called from an insecure page that doesn't use </span><code class=""><span>https</span></code><span>.</span></li><li><span>An incorrect payment request is passed. Payment requests are incorrect if they contain missing, unknown or invalid properties, or if the total amount is negative.</span></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Safari calls the</span><code class=""><span>onpaymentauthorized</span></code><span>callback with an</span><code class=""><span>event</span></code><span>object. The </span><code class=""><span>event</span></code><span> object passes a</span><code class=""><span>token</span></code><span>which you need to send to PayPal to confirm the order.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Capture the order using the  </span><a href="/api/orders/v2" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" target="" pa-marked="1" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>PayPal Orders V2 API</span></a><span>. Use </span><code class=""><span>paypal.Applepay().confirmOrder()</span></code><span> to send the </span><code class=""><span>orderID</span></code><span>, the Apple Pay token, billing contact details, and confirm the order.</span></p></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><div class="dx-anchor newArchetype numberedWrapper"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">6</span><h2 id="show-the-payment-sheet" class="dx-anchor newArchetype"> <span id="#show-the-payment-sheet" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#show-the-payment-sheet" class="dx-anchor__icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Show the payment sheet</h2></div></div></div><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>After you have created the Apple Pay session and added the callbacks, call the </span><code class=""><span>session.begin</span></code><span>method to show the payment sheet. You can only call the</span><code class=""><span>begin</span></code><span>method when a buyer explicitly requests a payment, such as inside an</span><code class=""><span>onclick</span></code><span>event. The </span><code class=""><span>begin</span></code><span> method throws a JavaScript exception if the buyer does not explicitly request the action:</span></p></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">session</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">.</span><span class="token method function property-access" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">begin</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">;</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="codeContent"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>After the buyer starts a payment in the browser, they use their Apple device to authorize the payment.</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="customize-payment" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#customize-payment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#customize-payment" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-customizepayment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-customizepayment" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Customize payment</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Customize the payment experience using the
      </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/apple_pay_on_the_web" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Apple Pay JavaScript SDK</span></a><span>.
</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Per Apple's development guidelines, your Apple Pay integration needs to follow these rules:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>The last step of an Apple Pay transaction should be when the buyer uses the payment sheet to confirm the payment.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Don't ask the buyer to complete additional confirmation after they use the Apple Pay payment sheet to confirm the payment.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Don't allow changes to the order after the buyer confirms the payment on the Apple Pay payment sheet.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><span>The commonly used customizations for Apple Pay are:</span></p><span>
</span><style data-emotion="css 48px);}}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr{background-color:#ffffff;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr transparent;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr >td{padding:0.75rem;}.css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100 >tbody >tr </table></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="test-your-integration" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">7</span><h2 id="test-your-integration" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#test-your-integration" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#test-your-integration" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Test your integration</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Test your Apple Pay integration in the PayPal sandbox and production environments to ensure that your app works correctly.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Use your personal sandbox login information during checkout to complete a payment using Apple Pay. Then, log into the sandbox site </span><a href="https://sandbox.paypal.com" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>sandbox.paypal.com</span></a><span> to see that the money has moved into your account.</span></p><span>
</span><ol><li><span>Open your test page with the Safari web browser on an iOS device or computer.</span></li><li><span>Get a test card from your Apple sandbox account.</span></li><li><span>Add the test card to your Apple Wallet on your iOS device or by using the Safari browser on the web.</span></li><li><span>Tap the </span><span class="boldText"><span>Apple Pay</span></span><span> button to open a pop-up with the Apple Pay payment sheet.</span></li><li><span>Make a payment using the Apple Pay payment sheet.</span></li><li><span>If you have an additional confirmation page on your merchant website, continue to confirm the payment.</span></li><li><span>Log in to your merchant account and continue to your confirmation page to confirm that the money you used for payment showed up in the account.</span></li></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="go-live" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">8</span><h2 id="go-live" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#go-live" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#go-live" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Go live</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Make Apple Pay available to buyers using your website or app.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><b><span>Important: </span></b><span>Before going live, complete </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/bizsignup/add-product?product=payment_methods&amp;capabilities=APPLE_PAY" class="dx-external-href linkFormat dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>production onboarding</span></a><span> to process Apple Pay payments with your live PayPal account.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3 id="live-environment" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#live-environment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#live-environment" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-liveenvironment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-liveenvironment" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Live environment</h3><span>
</span><p><span>If you're a new merchant, sign up for a  </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/business" class="linkFormat dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>PayPal business account</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Use your personal production login information during checkout to complete an Apple Pay transaction. Then log into </span><b><span>paypal.com</span></b><span> to see the money move out of your account.</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="getting-started-in-your-live-environment" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#getting-started-in-your-live-environment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#getting-started-in-your-live-environment" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <span id="link-gettingstartedinyourliveenvironment" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span><a tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" href="#link-gettingstartedinyourliveenvironment" class="dx-anchor__icon" pa-marked="1"></a> Getting started in your live environment</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Verify any domain names in your live environment that will show an Apple Pay button. Apple Pay transactions only work on a domain and site registered to you.</span></p><span>
</span><ul><li><a href="#download-host" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Download and host</span></a><span>  the domain association file for your live environment.</span></li><li><a href="#register-your-live-domain" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Register your live domain</span></a><span>  on your PayPal Developer Dashboard.</span></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><b><span>Important: </span></b><span>The Apple Pay payment method won't work if the domain and site aren't registered. The merchant that owns the domain is responsible for registering that domain.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p id="download-host"><b><span>Prerequisites</span></b></p><span>
</span><p><span>Enable Apple Pay for your live account:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Log into the PayPal Developer Dashboard with your live PayPal account.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the </span><span class="boldText"><span>Sandbox/Live</span></span><span> toggle so it shows </span><span class="boldText"><span>Live</span></span><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Go to </span><span class="boldText"><span>Apps & Credentials</span></span><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Scroll down to </span><span class="boldText"><span>Features</span></span><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the </span><span class="boldText"><span>Apple Pay</span></span><span> checkbox and select the </span><span class="boldText"><span>Save</span></span><span> link.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><span>Create an app:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Log into the PayPal Developer Dashboard with your live PayPal account.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the </span><span class="boldText"><span>Sandbox/Live</span></span><span> toggle so it shows </span><span class="boldText"><span>Live</span></span><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Go to </span><span class="boldText"><span>Apps & Credentials</span></span><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Create an app similar to what you created in the sandbox. You don't need to log into a separate test account.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p id="download-host"><b><span>Download and host live domain association file</span></b></p><span>
</span><p><span>Host a domain association file for each high-level domain and subdomain that show the Apple Pay button.</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Download the domain association file for your live environment.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Host the file on your live site for each domain and subdomain you want to register, at </span><code class=""><span>/.well-known/apple-developer-merchantid-domain-association</span></code><span>. For example:</span><ul><span>
            </span><li><code class=""><span>https://example.com/.well-known/apple-developer-merchantid-domain-association</span></code></li><span>
            </span><li><code class=""><span>https://subdomain.example.com/.well-known/apple-developer-merchantid-domain-association</span></code></li><span>
        </span></ul><span>
    </span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><a href="https://paypalobjects.com/devdoc/apple-pay/well-known/apple-developer-merchantid-domain-association" class="css-1m0ekac-button_base-text_button_lg-btn_full_width dx-external-href dx-external-href" role="button" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ppui-info="buttons_7.9.9" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>Download</span></a></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><b><span>Note: </span></b><span>Remove the file extension from the domain association file when you host it on your server.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><strong><span>Register your live domain on PayPal</span></strong></p><span>
</span><p><span>Add all high-level domains that show the Apple Pay button.</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Log into the PayPal Developer Dashboard with your live PayPal account.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the Sandbox/Live toggle so it shows Live.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Go to Apps & Credentials.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select your app.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Scroll down to Features &gt; Accept payments &gt; Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Check if Apple Pay is enabled. If Apple Pay isn't enabled, select the Apple Pay checkbox and select the Save link to enable Apple Pay.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the Manage link in the Apple Pay section.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select Add Domain and enter your domain name.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select Register Domain. If registration fails, check that the domain association file is live and saved to the right place on your live site.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><strong><span>Note:</span></strong><span> When Apple verifies a domain, it makes a request to retrieve the domain verification file. Ensure that:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>The file is not served with a </span><code class=""><span>3XX</span></code><span> status code. Apple does not support HTTP URL redirects for the domain association file.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>This file is served via HTTPS 1.1.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><strong><span>Important:</span></strong><span> This file is served with </span><code class=""><span>Content-Type: application/octet-stream</span></code><span> to indicate that this is a binary file download.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The HTTP response for this request returns this file as a binary object and not as HTML, or plain text.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Access to this file is not behind a firewall. See </span><a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/apple_pay_on_the_web/setting_up_your_server" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Apple documentation</span></a><span> on allowing Apple IP addresses.</span></li><span>
</span></ul></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><span>
</span><p><span>After your domain is registered:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>The domain appears under </span><strong><span>Domains registered with Apple Pay</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Buyers can make payments using the Apple Pay button on the registered website.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><h2>Testing in your live environment</h2><span>
</span><p><span>When testing a purchase in production, consider:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>The business account receiving money can't also make the purchase.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>If you create a personal account with the same information as the business account, those accounts might experience restrictions.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><span>How to test Apple Pay payments in a live environment:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Open your test page with Safari on iOS or desktop.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Select the Apple Pay button to open a pop-up with the Apple Pay payment sheet.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Proceed with the Apple Pay checkout transaction.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>If you have an additional confirmation page on your merchant website, confirm the payment.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Log in to your merchant account and confirm that the money has moved into that account.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><h2>Troubleshoot your integration</h2><span>
</span><p><span>Make sure that there are no browser console warnings or errors. The JavaScript SDK configuration attributes have distinct validation checks for input formatting and values.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>If the validation fails, the web browser's developer console shows warning messages that say which property is incorrect and what you need to do to address the issue. The library generally attempts to revert to the safe default values if missing or incorrect inputs exist.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="next-steps-&amp;-customizations" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="secondaryBackground"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div style="display:block;margin-top:8px;width:100%"><p style="margin-top:8px;margin-bottom:8px">Get started testing, add security to your checkout experience or create customizations for your </span></p><p><span>Add PayPal payment buttons and customized card fields.</span></p></div></div></div><footer class="css-1ygyq7k-footer" data-ppui="true"></footer></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="footerWrapper"><div class="Footer-module_pp-footer__OHeGT"><a href="/reference/">Reference</a><a href="https://www.paypal.com">PayPal.com</a><a href="https://www.paypal.com/myaccount/privacy/privacyhub?_ga=1.14097599.947497879.1704302180">Privacy</a><a href="https://www.paypal.com/myaccount/privacy/cookiePrefs?_ga=1.20912176.947497879.1704302180">Cookies</a><a href="/support/">Support</a><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/webapps/mpp/ua/legalhub-full?_ga=1.20912176.947497879.1704302180">Legal</a><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/smarthelp/contact-us?_ga=1.20912176.947497879.1704302180">Contact</a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><script src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/pa/js/min/pa.js"></script><script nonce="j3LuTSaOjkAY21qRtm8rbswzsqzD4VFIDsNvfgXbm6kdS0Ph">((STORAGE_KEY, restoreKey) => {

    }
    try {
      let positions = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) || "{}");
      let storedY = positions[restoreKey || window.history.state.key];
      if (typeof storedY === "number") {
        window.scrollTo(0, storedY);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
      sessionStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    }

"},{"node":"element","tag":"li","child":[{"node":"text","text":"If you have an additional confirmation page on your merchant website, confirm the payment."}]},{"node":"text","text":"\n    "},{"node":"element","tag":"li","child":[{"node":"text","text":"Log in to your merchant account and confirm that the money has moved into that
